Yes, this is true. But discrimination grows through exercise and control. In other words, you ask me if what you have observed is correct, and with the help of my answers you can rectify your observations.<span class='page-number' id='s-37' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/37.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.37]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 May 1934
# /cwm/17/18-may-1934


## 18 May 1934

*This morning Z asked me, "Why didn't X drink his cocoa and why is he taking a walk?" I told her what I thought about it.*<span class='page-number' id='s-37' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/37.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.37]</a></span>

Speaking about others is not only useless but most often harmful.

*But why seek to know the motives of other people's actions? I don't know what to do in such cases. If someone asks me, I simply have to answer.*

You can always say, "Mother does not like us to gossip about others."<span class='page-number' id='s-38' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/38.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.38]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 May 1934
# /cwm/17/18-may-1934-1


## 18 May 1934

*But it all depends on the person we tell this to. What if he rebels?*

So much the worse for him!

*What should I do so as not to open myself to vital contacts?*

Fix your consciousness higher than the vital.<span class='page-number' id='s-38' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/38.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.38]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 May 1934
# /cwm/17/21-may-1934


## 21 May 1934

*I have decided to smile only at a few people and never at a woman. Is this all right?*

Always to maintain an attitude of concentration on the Divine Life is more important than making rules that are too rigid. It would be better to resolve not to smile in expectation of a vital interchange.<span class='page-number' id='s-38' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/38.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.38]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 May 1934
# /cwm/17/21-may-1934-1


## 21 May 1934

*Isn't it true that one should know all one's impurities?*

Knowing them is indeed necessary, but it is not good to fix one's<span class='page-number' id='s-38' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/38.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.38]</a></span> attention too constantly on them; it does not help to remove them—on the contrary.<span class='page-number' id='s-39' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/39.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.39]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 May 1934
# /cwm/17/22-may-1934


## 22 May 1934

*Z asked me, "What is that?" I replied, "Mother wrote something to me for my birthday." "May I see it?" she said. I let her read it. I don't think I did the right thing.*

Obviously, when I give a prayer on such an occasion I concentrate a certain force in it. By showing the prayer to others you destroy a great deal of the effect of this force.<span class='page-number' id='s-39' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/39.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.39]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 May 1934
# /cwm/17/23-may-1934


## 23 May 1934

*I think there is also some force in your letters, so it is better not to show them to anyone.*

Yes, and as a rule I do not like answering questions about others. In yoga each one should attend to his own progress—the progress of others has nothing to do with him.<span class='page-number' id='s-39' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/39.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.39]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 May 1934
# /cwm/17/23-may-1934-1


## 23 May 1934

*Isn't it better to tell you the ideas we have about someone so that you can correct them? Because if they are wrong, it is very dangerous.*

Certainly, and the best thing is precisely to refrain from all ideas about people, for then there isn't any risk of having wrong ideas.

*Of course, the best thing is not to have any ideas about people, but I don't think this is possible until the mind is purified.*<span class='page-number' id='s-39' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/39.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.39]</a></span>

Yes, it is quite possible if the mind is interested and engrossed in something more useful.<span class='page-number' id='s-40' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/40.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.40]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 May 1934
# /cwm/17/24-may-1934


## 24 May 1934

*So it would be better to reject the ideas I have about others and stop making mental constructions about people?*

Yes, it is preferable.

*Is it good for me to see X?*

That depends on what you mean by *seeing* him; if it is to exchange a few words or to do some work together from time to time, it does not matter. But long conversations should be avoided.<span class='page-number' id='s-40' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/40.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.40]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 May 1934
# /cwm/17/24-may-1934-1


## 24 May 1934

*What pleasure does one get out of making fun of others?*

Indeed, I fail to see what pleasure one finds in hurting other people's feelings. It is not nice and shows so much pretentious foolishness.<span class='page-number' id='s-40' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/40.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.40]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 May 1934
# /cwm/17/25-may-1934


## 25 May 1934

*Was it right to write this to you: "A man like Y thinks he is very disciplined. Where is his discipline when he talks like this?" Aren't my last words exaggerated?*

They may not be exaggerated, but in any case they are not very kind, and kindness is an indispensable step towards the widening and illumination of the consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-40' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/40.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.40]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 May 1934
# /cwm/17/26-may-1934


## 26 May 1934

*Sweet Mother! When will the vital yearn for the Divine? May its passion be changed into psychic love, its anger into*

Equanimity

*its jealousy into*

Trust

*its vanity into*

Modesty

*its selfishness into*

Self-giving.<span class='page-number' id='s-41' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/41.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.41]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 May 1934
# /cwm/17/26-may-1934-1


## 26 May 1934

*X used to go home with me after lunch, but yesterday he left without me. He told me that he didn't have any reason for doing so. Is it true?*

It is quite possible that he left without any reason. One does so many things without any conscious motive.<span class='page-number' id='s-41' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/41.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.41]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 May 1934
# /cwm/17/28-may-1934


## 28 May 1934

*You wrote that one does so many things without any conscious motive. But is that really desirable? I think it is better not to do anything without thinking it over carefully.*

Certainly, that is preferable.<span class='page-number' id='s-41' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/41.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.41]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 May 1934
# /cwm/17/29-may-1934


## 29 May 1934

*A dream: It was night, I was writing a poem. Suddenly Y came and put out the kerosene lamp on the table. A little later she also switched off the electric light. Does this dream have any significance?*

If the dream has a significance (which is not sure), it would mean that a certain type of hostile force took the likeness of Y in your consciousness. Lights going out are always the symbol of the consciousness descending into unconsciousness.

*Sweet Mother, I would like to know why my consciousness is going outwards and also why my aspiration has diminished.*

Probably a part of your nature which is not yet converted has risen to the surface and is active at present.<span class='page-number' id='s-42' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/42.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.42]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 May 1934
# /cwm/17/29-may-1934-1


## 29 May 1934

*So what should I do when an unconverted part rises to the surface?*

Put the light and the knowledge on it patiently until it gets converted.<span class='page-number' id='s-42' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/42.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.42]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 May 1934
# /cwm/17/30-may-1934


## 30 May 1934

*Mother, you wrote that I should put the light and the knowledge on the unconverted part until it gets converted. I think it is You who can do that.*

That is exactly what I mean; you have only to call Sri Aurobindo or myself and ask that this obscure part be enlightened and converted.<span class='page-number' id='s-42' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/42.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.42]</a></span>


# Chapter: 31 May 1934
# /cwm/17/31-may-1934


## 31 May 1934

*Z often asks me questions about grammar. I don't know French well, so it would be better if he didn't ask.*

What little you do know, you can tell to others, but take care to warn them that you do not know much and that you are not sure of the correctness of your answers.<span class='page-number' id='s-43' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/43.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.43]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 June 1934
# /cwm/17/1-june-1934


## 1 June 1934

*Is it good to go to the temple? The idea came to me that if one believes in the Divine without form, one will not believe in the Divine with form—as a human being, I mean.*

You mean: if one has faith in the god of a religion, how can one have faith in the incarnate Divine? That is quite right.<span class='page-number' id='s-43' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/43.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.43]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 June 1934
# /cwm/17/2-june-1934


## 2 June 1934

*May I take the geography books home? I won't let them out of my room.*

Yes, you may take the geography books, but you must take great care of them so that they don't get torn or stained or eaten by insects.<span class='page-number' id='s-43' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/43.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.43]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 June 1934
# /cwm/17/4-june-1934


## 4 June 1934

*I don't understand why and how X has had difficulties because of affection. I haven't had them. Perhaps it is because I am not aware of them.*

It is because affection creates an attachment in him, and all attachment is contrary to Yoga.<span class='page-number' id='s-43' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/43.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.43]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 June 1934
# /cwm/17/4-june-1934-1


## 4 June 1934

*Does affection create attachment in me?*

Affection always creates attachment, unless one is a yogi.

*It seems that there is no electricity in the vital world—the dreams are always dark.*

Who told you this extraordinary tale?

Certainly there is no electricity such as men use in the physical world. But there are as many lights as one could wish for—even most beautiful, most brilliant ones, so that unless one is forewarned one might believe oneself to be on a very high plane.<span class='page-number' id='s-44' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/44.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.44]</a></span>


# Chapter: 5 June 1934
# /cwm/17/5-june-1934


## 5 June 1934

*You say that there are as many lights in the vital world as one could wish for—but are they real lights or are they created by vital beings?*

The lights in the vital world are vital lights, of course.

*In my dreams I do not see daylight as I do here; I see everything very dim.*

That is because your vision is not fully developed in that world or because you go to dark places there. But that does not mean that the whole vital world is dark!<span class='page-number' id='s-44' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/44.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.44]</a></span>


# Chapter: 6 June 1934
# /cwm/17/6-june-1934


## 6 June 1934

*How can I keep the most enlightened part of my mind always on the surface?*

Will for it, and call on the enlightened part to intervene each time that the parts which are still obscure, ignorant and egoistic try to dominate your being.<span class='page-number' id='s-44' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/44.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.44]</a></span>

*Why is it that you do not answer certain questions? Is it because the question is not sincere?*

Usually it is because the question is badly stated; often it is because it would not be good to reply.<span class='page-number' id='s-45' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/45.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.45]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 June 1934
# /cwm/17/9-june-1934


## 9 June 1934

*These last two days I have been feeling sad about my jealousy.*

Feeling sad is of no use. All the energy you waste in feeling sad would better be used in transforming the wrong movement.

*But this morning, after my pranam, I felt very happy. Is it impossible for the ordinary mind to turn easily towards the Divine, even when there is an intense aspiration?*

There is nothing impossible about a prompt conversion; the difficult thing is to make it last.<span class='page-number' id='s-45' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/45.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.45]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1934
# /cwm/17/11-june-1934


## 11 June 1934

*Often when there is something to be done, two answers come. One part says not to do it, the other says there is no harm in it. Who decides which part is wrong and which is right?*

If the psychic consciousness were fully awakened, it would decide. But in this case it is one part of the mind arguing with another and, at best, it is the mental Purusha that steps in and decides.<span class='page-number' id='s-45' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/45.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.45]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1934
# /cwm/17/11-june-1934-1


## 11 June 1934

*I don't quite understand what you mean by "There is nothing impossible about a prompt conversion; the difficult thing is to make it last." It gets converted for a moment and then falls back again?*

Yes. The mind suddenly sees clearly and is converted, but then it is attacked again by obscurity and falls back into its old habits.

*How can the conversion of the ordinary mind be made lasting?*

Persist in bringing it into contact with the light until the conversion becomes lasting.<span class='page-number' id='s-46' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/46.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.46]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1934
# /cwm/17/11-june-1934-2


## 11 June 1934

*It seems that women have a power of attraction which they throw upon men—a natural movement—and that men are caught like fish in a net and often unable to escape. Is this true? What is the way to avoid being touched by this power, or what must we do to escape from it?*

I think it is a mutual effect—and women complain that men do the same thing to them. The remedy is to turn the consciousness towards the Divine alone.<span class='page-number' id='s-46' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/46.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.46]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 June 1934
# /cwm/17/26-june-1934


## 26 June 1934

*Y told me that it is very good to take tea or coffee when one has a sore throat and that he takes it two or three times a day.*

Each one has his own remedies and habits, which may be good<span class='page-number' id='s-46' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/46.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.46]</a></span> for him, but it would be a great mistake to generalise and try to apply them to other people.<span class='page-number' id='s-47' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/47.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.47]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 June 1934
# /cwm/17/28-june-1934


## 28 June 1934

*I spent nearly three-quarters of the night awake. I think that visions are preventing me from sleeping.*

In any case, it is the restless and unquiet vital.<span class='page-number' id='s-47' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/47.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.47]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 June 1934
# /cwm/17/28-june-1934-1


## 28 June 1934

*This afternoon I slept from 12:30 to 3:30; that is too long, I think.*

No, it is all right since you are sleeping very badly.<span class='page-number' id='s-47' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/47.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.47]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 June 1934
# /cwm/17/28-june-1934-2


## 28 June 1934

*How can I calm the vital so as to sleep better? By aspiration?*

And a concentration, a will to reject the restlessness.

*As for deciding about ghosts, I would like to know which part it is that doubts the reasoning of the other parts.*

These are various fragments of the mind opposing and contradicting one another, and they are not all at the same stage of development.<span class='page-number' id='s-47' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/47.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.47]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 June 1934
# /cwm/17/29-june-1934


## 29 June 1934

*It would be very interesting to become conscious of anti-divine ghosts.*

So long as it is in order to reject or conquer them.<span class='page-number' id='s-48' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/48.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.48]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 June 1934
# /cwm/17/29-june-1934-1


## 29 June 1934

*There are ghosts who try to lead us astray, but aren't there also ghosts who help us in our sadhana?*

I thought you were using the word "ghosts" to mean vital entities. Those beings are certainly not the ones who can help you in your sadhana.

*I would like to know how to conquer these anti-divine ghosts.*

By willing to do so, and by always refusing to believe in their suggestions.<span class='page-number' id='s-48' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/48.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.48]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 June 1934
# /cwm/17/30-june-1934


## 30 June 1934

*Yes, Mother, these vital entities lead us astray; but aren't there beings who can help us, lead us back to the right path?*

Yes, they do exist, but since they do not belong to the vital world that is nearest to the physical, it is more difficult for them to enter into contact with human beings. Their action is sometimes perceptible in the mind, and in the psychic it is very clear.

*In a dream, I was gathering flowers in the garden of my house. Suddenly the gate opened and three ladies came in. One lady asked me for flowers. I answered her, "All the beautiful flowers will be sent to the Mother. You can<span class='page-number' id='s-48' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/48.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.48]</a></span> take the ones that are not beautiful." But these ladies disturbed me.*

This is probably the symbol of certain forces of the lower nature trying to seize hold of what is already given to the Divine.<span class='page-number' id='s-49' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/49.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.49]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 July 1934
# /cwm/17/2-july-1934


## 2 July 1934

*Yesterday I was in a very strange state: for five minutes I felt bad, then five minutes later I felt joyful, and so on for three hours. Then I understood the whole game and I rejected it by will-power and prayer. But I really don't understand this movement.*

Two parts of the vital being were struggling together, each one in turn getting the upper hand.

*Z told me that in the mental and vital worlds there are beings who are against the anti-divine entities and who help us.*

Just as there are people on earth who like to help others.<span class='page-number' id='s-49' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/49.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.49]</a></span>


# Chapter: 3 July 1934
# /cwm/17/3-july-1934


## 3 July 1934

*Today I feel happy. I would like to know whether this happiness is spiritual or not.*

Instead of asking yourself such questions, it would be better to remain very quiet, concentrated and calm, so that the happiness may last.<span class='page-number' id='s-49' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/49.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.49]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 July 1934
# /cwm/17/4-july-1934


## 4 July 1934

*O Sweet Mother, teach me to remain unshakable when<span class='page-number' id='s-49' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/49.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.49]</a></span> someone talks to me, because afterwards my mind wanders.*

Do not identify yourself with the conversation. Watch it all from above and from a distance, as if someone else were listening and speaking, and say no more than is absolutely indispensable.<span class='page-number' id='s-50' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/50.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.50]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 July 1934
# /cwm/17/4-july-1934-1


## 4 July 1934

*Today I experienced the force working in me. I wonder how I did such a hard work—digging for a whole hour without taking any rest. But I don't understand why some trembling remained even after the work was over.*

The force was probably a bit too much for the body, which found it difficult to bear—hence the trembling.

*You wrote to me: "Say no more than is absolutely indispensable." But what should I do when someone asks me an unnecessary question?*

Just answer evasively with a word or two, without attaching any importance to it.<span class='page-number' id='s-50' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/50.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.50]</a></span>


# Chapter: 5 July 1934
# /cwm/17/5-july-1934


## 5 July 1934

*How can I prepare my body to bear Your force, Sweet Mother?*

The power to bear is found in calm and quietness.<span class='page-number' id='s-50' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/50.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.50]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 July 1934
# /cwm/17/9-july-1934


## 9 July 1934

*X told me that it is very good to read Sri Aurobindo's messages on doubt. "It is not at all necessary to read<span class='page-number' id='s-50' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/50.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.50]</a></span> about doubt," I answered him. "At this stage I don't think it is possible to be free from all doubt," he said.*

It is not only quite possible to be free of all doubt, it is an absolutely indispensable condition; but before being able to state with assurance that one is free from doubt, one should wait for a few months at least, in order to make sure.

In any case this kind of discussion is quite useless—it does not help to overcome doubt.<span class='page-number' id='s-51' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/51.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.51]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 July 1934
# /cwm/17/11-july-1934


## 11 July 1934

*Remove all weakness from me. It is not as easy as people think, Divine Mother, to become Your child integrally and perfectly. To do so one must...*

Be very sincere and straightforward, tolerate nothing in yourself that you could not show me without fear, and do nothing that you would feel ashamed of doing before me.<span class='page-number' id='s-51' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/51.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.51]</a></span>


# Chapter: 12 July 1934
# /cwm/17/12-july-1934


## 12 July 1934

*It seems that there is an ego in each state of consciousness; for example: mental ego, vital ego, physical ego.*

There is also a spiritual ego, and even the gods who live in the Overmind have their egos.

*And each one must be freed from his ego in order to attain the divine bliss.*

It is not enough to surrender; the ego must be dissolved, must merge with the Divine, disappear in Him.<span class='page-number' id='s-51' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/51.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.51]</a></span>


# Chapter: 12 July 1934
# /cwm/17/12-july-1934-1


## 12 July 1934

*I think that the Supramental Gods have no ego. So I believe that we must become egoless like them, on earth itself, and then act according to the divine guidance.*

I think it is useless to speculate just now about what may happen in the Supermind.<span class='page-number' id='s-52' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/52.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.52]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 July 1934
# /cwm/17/14-july-1934


## 14 July 1934

*At five o'clock I got ready to go and watch the Republic Day celebrations from the terrace of Aroumé. But thinking that You would prefer that I didn't go, I came back.*

I have no preference in this or in any other matter. For each person the decision depends on his own need.<span class='page-number' id='s-52' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/52.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.52]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 July 1934
# /cwm/17/16-july-1934


## 16 July 1934

*I don't understand what you mean by "I have no preference..." Does it mean that we have to decide for ourselves whether the thing is to be done or not, without asking You?*

No. I did not complete the sentence. I meant that I do not decide according to *preferences*, but according to each one's need.<span class='page-number' id='s-52' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/52.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.52]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 July 1934
# /cwm/17/23-july-1934


## 23 July 1934

*Mother, it wasn't an explanation that my sister asked me for last time, but something about one of Sri Aurobindo's letters. When I read what she had written about the material world, about leaving her house, I was disturbed—hence the obstacle to my aspiration. My Sweet Mother, I will do as You wish.*<span class='page-number' id='s-52' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/52.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.52]</a></span>

If it disturbs you, you need not listen to what she says or explain Sri Aurobindo's letters to her.

*This evening I gave her an explanation without feeling disturbed.*

But obviously it is much better if you can overcome the weakness that makes you feel disturbed, because that is the true cure.<span class='page-number' id='s-53' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/53.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.53]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 July 1934
# /cwm/17/24-july-1934


## 24 July 1934

*My sweet little Mother,*

*Yesterday evening during the meditation I felt so much love—I felt waves, vibrations of love. But this love pours itself out on others. Before, when I felt a lot of love it remained silent; I became more serious and I did not express it. But this time, on the contrary, I allowed the love to express itself because I don't find it undesirable. But if You think it necessary, I will turn it inwards.*

The love that one contains in silence acts within oneself for purification and transformation. The love that one turns outwards—if one does it in a pure and disinterested way—may occasionally help others. But most often they receive it wrongly... So you must do as your instinct guides you.<span class='page-number' id='s-53' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/53.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.53]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 July 1934
# /cwm/17/24-july-1934-1


## 24 July 1934

*Today I spoke to twenty-four people; it is too much, I think. Since this morning I have been feeling a lack of happiness; there is no bad feeling, but the love I felt is no longer there.*

That is quite natural—you have wasted it right and left; instead<span class='page-number' id='s-53' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/53.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.53]</a></span> of concentrating on the Divine what came from the Divine, you have squandered it on others and lost it.<span class='page-number' id='s-54' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/54.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.54]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 July 1934
# /cwm/17/24-july-1934-2


## 24 July 1934

*After reading your reply, Sweet Mother, I became serious. I thought that I should keep silent, at least for today. A moment later another part of my being said, "It is not a real silence but rather a dissatisfaction of the vital, for you can very well see that there is not much happiness and enthusiasm in it." I thought that the second part was right.*

Both are partly true and partly false. It is wise to receive the descending Force in silence and concentration, but this silence and concentration should not come from the vital's resentment at not being allowed to follow its whims.

This concentration and silence should not only be full of a *great peace* but also of a *very intense happiness.* Then one knows that the movement is true and unmixed.<span class='page-number' id='s-54' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/54.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.54]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 July 1934
# /cwm/17/28-july-1934


## 28 July 1934

*O Mother, I want to become Your perfectly obedient child, I want to know Your will before You express it. To achieve that I must...*

Have no preference about anything except to carry out the divine will.<span class='page-number' id='s-54' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/54.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.54]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 July 1934
# /cwm/17/1-july-1934


## 1 July 1934

*Will You tell me, Mother, what to do to get rid of egoism?*<span class='page-number' id='s-54' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/54.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.54]</a></span>

One achieves it by persistently willing it.<span class='page-number' id='s-55' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/55.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.55]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 August 1934
# /cwm/17/1-august-1934


## 1 August 1934

*My sweet Mother, in a dream I saw You in various forms. You were very young, my age, about seventeen or eighteen, and yet I behaved towards You as if I were Your child. But I doubt very much whether this young girl I called Mother was anything more than a being taking on Your form.*

It is not at all impossible that I should appear in various forms, even in the form of a young girl.<span class='page-number' id='s-55' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/55.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.55]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 August 1934
# /cwm/17/1-august-1934-1


## 1 August 1934

*I don't understand, Mother, why I so often see scorpions and snakes in my dreams.*

They are symbols of bad thoughts and perverted or obscure energies.<span class='page-number' id='s-55' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/55.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.55]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 August 1934
# /cwm/17/2-august-1934


## 2 August 1934

*Mother, I don't know what to do about my studies when there is a pressure, because my mind stops working.*

Just wait until your mind starts working again.<span class='page-number' id='s-55' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/55.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.55]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 August 1934
# /cwm/17/18-august-1934


## 18 August 1934

*This evening I talked unnecessarily, so that when You came I felt nothing.*

When I saw you as I left, your atmosphere was very agitated and your consciousness quite superficial. I could clearly<span class='page-number' id='s-55' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/55.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.55]</a></span> see that contact with all those women is not doing you any good.<span class='page-number' id='s-56' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/56.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.56]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 August 1934
# /cwm/17/20-august-1934


## 20 August 1934

*Certainly I have no doubt that one day I will have love, but how can I spend even a day without love? Better to die than to remain without love for You—that is the suggestion that came to me.*

That is absurd.

It is not by dying but by living that one can realise love.<span class='page-number' id='s-56' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/56.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.56]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 August 1934
# /cwm/17/22-august-1934


## 22 August 1934

*Everywhere in me I see nothing but obscurity and ignorance. When will I stop wasting time? Where are my obedience and my sincerity? Where is the peace, the happiness? Why has my zeal dried up? Where am I, Mother?*

It is no use getting upset or tormenting yourself. Only in peace and calm can the good experience return.<span class='page-number' id='s-56' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/56.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.56]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 August 1934
# /cwm/17/23-august-1934


## 23 August 1934

*Will you tell me something about relationships with other people, because it is not fully clear to me.*

It is impossible to give any external rule, since each case should receive its own particular solution. The inner attitude must be *true* and perfectly sincere.<span class='page-number' id='s-56' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/56.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.56]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 August 1934
# /cwm/17/25-august-1934


## 25 August 1934

*You wrote to me, concerning relationships with others, "The inner attitude must be true and perfectly sincere." Since I don't have this attitude yet, I think it would be better not to associate with anyone and wait until it comes.*

You must make an effort to attain this attitude—waiting is not enough.<span class='page-number' id='s-57' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/57.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.57]</a></span>


# Chapter: 27 August 1934
# /cwm/17/27-august-1934


## 27 August 1934

*Isn't my attitude towards Y undesirable? Sometimes I tease her by giving her flowers.*

I cannot see any benefit in these familiarities—surely they do not help to raise the consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-57' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/57.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.57]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 August 1934
# /cwm/17/30-august-1934


## 30 August 1934

*Somebody said that the monthly review "The Theosophical Path" helped Sri Aurobindo a lot.*

What nonsense is this!!

Can Sri Aurobindo be helped by anyone or anything? It is *He who helps*, he is not helped!

*When I came out of Z's house the love and happiness in me had disappeared. Besides, this is not the first time I have been disturbed by contact with her. So I got the idea to stop seeing her.*

After so often having the same experience of losing everything there, I cannot understand why you continue to go!

*Normally what happens when You do not reply is that there is a struggle between two parts of the mind.*<span class='page-number' id='s-57' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/57.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.57]</a></span>

When I do not reply, it is because it is neither good nor bad, true nor false, and it would take too long to explain the truth.

*Give me Your love, Mother.*

I give it to you constantly, but you must not always lose it by continually repeating the same mistakes.<span class='page-number' id='s-58' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/58.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.58]</a></span>


# Chapter: 31 August 1934
# /cwm/17/31-august-1934


## 31 August 1934

*Please tell me what to do, Mother, so that nothing and no one can disturb me.*

The whole being must be governed by the psychic being and by that alone.<span class='page-number' id='s-58' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/58.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.58]</a></span>


# Chapter: 5 September 1934
# /cwm/17/5-september-1934


## 5 September 1934

*I don't know what to do, for my being has been under attack since last night. At the moment I feel restless, depressed, in darkness and ignorance. Above all, consciousness is absent.*

The less importance one attaches to these dark periods, the sooner they are over.<span class='page-number' id='s-58' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/58.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.58]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 September 1934
# /cwm/17/10-september-1934


## 10 September 1934

*Where is my consciousness at the moment! What is the nature of this depression and why is it lasting so long? Before, Mother, Your force would come and drive it away. Where is that force now? Alas! I have lost it.*

Be calm and quiet; it is only a crisis which will pass with the increase of consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-58' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/58.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.58]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 September 1934
# /cwm/17/11-september-1934


## 11 September 1934

*Sweet Mother, I feel that I am doing something against Your will. This unknown thing is hostile and makes me feel bad.*

I am not aware of anything special that is being done against my will. But you must not let yourself be disturbed. You must will to become more and more honest and sincere, and, for the rest, rely on the divine Grace.<span class='page-number' id='s-59' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/59.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.59]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 September 1934
# /cwm/17/14-september-1934


## 14 September 1934

*The mind wants to know how this crisis came and why it has remained so long. What should one do when this happens?*

It has been quite a widespread attack. When this happens, the best thing is to remain quiet without getting agitated either inwardly or outwardly.<span class='page-number' id='s-59' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/59.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.59]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 September 1934
# /cwm/17/15-september-1934


## 15 September 1934

*Even when I am in a good state of consciousness, the mind is not always at peace. There are all kinds of random thoughts.*

It is behind the mind, behind the vital, in the psychic centre that one can find the quietness that never wavers.<span class='page-number' id='s-59' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/59.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.59]</a></span>


# Chapter: 17 September 1934
# /cwm/17/17-september-1934


## 17 September 1934

*The pressure is constantly there. Grant me quietness, my sweet Mother.*

I never cease pouring peace and quietness and calm on you why don't you accept them?<span class='page-number' id='s-59' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/59.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.59]</a></span>


# Chapter: 17 September 1934
# /cwm/17/17-september-1934-1


## 17 September 1934

*What must I do to accept the peace and quietness and calm?*

Want them sincerely and integrally—not only with one part of your being.

*Last night I talked with X until 11:40, But in spite of that—no sleep!*

Staying up late is surely not the way to prepare yourself to sleep well.<span class='page-number' id='s-60' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/60.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.60]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 September 1934
# /cwm/17/21-september-1934


## 21 September 1934

*I must have felt something during my pranam, because afterwards I wept. O my sweet Mother, why?*

Because during the pranam I reestablished the contact between your ordinary consciousness and the psychic consciousness.

The extreme sweetness of the psychic consciousness always makes the outer consciousness weep with emotion.<span class='page-number' id='s-60' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/60.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.60]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 September 1934
# /cwm/17/22-september-1934


## 22 September 1934

*For a long time I have been aspiring with all my heart, Mother, for You to grant me Your love and peace.*

My love and peace are always with you—it is for you to learn to receive them.<span class='page-number' id='s-60' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/60.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.60]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 September 1934
# /cwm/17/23-september-1934


## 23 September 1934

*This morning Y came up to me and I spoke freely with her. Then as I was speaking, I felt as if I were surrounded by fire. I felt feverish almost the whole day. All these<span class='page-number' id='s-60' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/60.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.60]</a></span> things come through contact with her, I think, so I ought to avoid her.*
 
Rather than avoiding this person or that, to no great effect, it would be so much better to change your consciousness, to close it to all these influences and keep it open only to the Divine!<span class='page-number' id='s-61' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/61.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.61]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 September 1934
# /cwm/17/26-september-1934


## 26 September 1934

*For several days I have been feeling that Z has an attraction for me. Since You wrote, "Rather than avoiding this person or that... ", I thought I could talk to her and thus gradually come to the true attitude.*

*Mother... love.*

If it is divine love that you mean, one can obtain it only by renouncing human love, which is a travesty and caricature of it.<span class='page-number' id='s-61' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/61.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.61]</a></span>


# Chapter: 27 September 1934
# /cwm/17/27-september-1934


## 27 September 1934

*O Mother, I want to act according to Your will and nothing else.*

Then quickly leave the path you have taken—do not waste your time wandering about and talking to girls. Start working in earnest again, study, educate yourself. occupy your mind with interesting and useful things rather than useless chit-chat, and do not give false excuses for your vital attractions. If your wish is truly sincere, you may be sure that you will have my force to help you to conquer.<span class='page-number' id='s-61' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/61.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.61]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 September 1934
# /cwm/17/29-september-1934


## 29 September 1934

*When will my being, which has gone astray, return to the path leading straight to You?*

Nothing could be easier—you have only to decide resolutely<span class='page-number' id='s-61' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/61.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.61]</a></span> that you want nothing but the divine life and turn away from everything else. You are sure to find me immediately.<span class='page-number' id='s-62' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/62.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.62]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 September 1934
# /cwm/17/29-september-1934-1


## 29 September 1934

*Because my nature is weak, it becomes difficult to renounce ordinary things. But it is sure that I want only You; if You are not there—death and nothing else.*

There is no question of dying. Leaving your body is not a solution; you remain with your desires and it is worse. It is much more reasonable and true to let your desires die, understanding how useless and stupid they are.

Since you want the Divine Life so much, you need not be afraid of failure, for a sincere and sustained aspiration is always fulfilled.

Make a firm resolution to overcome your weaknesses and you will see that it is not so difficult as it seems. My force is with you to overcome the obstacles, and also my blessings.<span class='page-number' id='s-62' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/62.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.62]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 October 1934
# /cwm/17/13-october-1934


## 13 October 1934

*Today I did not study. I still have a headache. I often lose courage and wish that the Sudarshan Chakra[^1] would come and put me to sleep for ever.*

[^1]: The lethal weapon of Sri Krishna.

To have so little courage at your age—it is shameful!

Rest if you are tired, but never lose the will for victory.<span class='page-number' id='s-62' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/62.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.62]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 October 1934
# /cwm/17/15-october-1934


## 15 October 1934

*I am very much interested in writing and reading stories. Then I forget the pain.*

Which proves that your pain is at least three-fourths imaginary.<span class='page-number' id='s-62' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/62.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.62]</a></span>

*So the only question about continuing to write or read like this, if You approve, is that of time—writing stories takes a lot of time.*

I see no harm in your reading and telling stories, but it should not interfere with your studies. Besides, to develop your style you can very well write any stories you please.<span class='page-number' id='s-63' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/63.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.63]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 October 1934
# /cwm/17/15-october-1934-1


## 15 October 1934

*O Mother, make me understand this imaginary illness. I don't understand it at all.*

You think that you are ill and that increases the illness. When you forget the illness, it goes away almost completely.<span class='page-number' id='s-63' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/63.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.63]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 October 1934
# /cwm/17/16-october-1934


## 16 October 1934

*This morning X offered me some betel. I told her that Mother forbids it. "No, one can take it sometimes," she said; "then you can wash your mouth before going to pranam."*

What hypocrisy!! IT IS SHAMEFUL.

*O Mother, how can one hope for Your love with such open disobedience! Why press others to act against Your will?*

Yes, it is very base. It is because of such actions, constantly repeated, that these people never make any progress.<span class='page-number' id='s-63' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/63.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.63]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 October 1934
# /cwm/17/18-october-1934


## 18 October 1934

*I think that illnesses of the physical body are mostly imaginary. So if one always remained outside the body,<span class='page-number' id='s-63' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/63.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.63]</a></span> as one does during sleep, probably one would never feel ill. It is only a matter of remaining outside the body.*

It is not remaining outside the body that cures illness. it is thinking in the true way and refusing everything in one's thought that could give support to the illness.<span class='page-number' id='s-64' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/64.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.64]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 October 1934
# /cwm/17/20-october-1934


## 20 October 1934

*My mind is busy from time to time with the story I have started writing. But is it good for it to be occupied in this way?*

It is better for it to be occupied with that, *if your story is interesting*, than with flirtation or nonsense.<span class='page-number' id='s-64' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/64.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.64]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 October 1934
# /cwm/17/20-october-1934-1


## 20 October 1934

*O Mother, why don't I feel Your love?*

Because you are looking for it in the wrong place, or under a false form.

*I feel that I am alone, wandering here and there.*

The vital must have decided that my love would express itself in a particular way, and as it did not happen that way, the vital says, "There is no love!"<span class='page-number' id='s-64' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/64.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.64]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 October 1934
# /cwm/17/23-october-1934


## 23 October 1934

*I think, Mother, that there are three states of consciousness for feeling Your love. In the first, a man is only an ordinary human being and feels nothing whether he sees You or not. In the second, he feels something if he does<span class='page-number' id='s-64' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/64.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.64]</a></span> not see You for a long time. In the third, he does not need Your physical body—in the extreme fire of love Your body and his physical body are dissolved in a soul-communion. I think, Mother, that man does not need Your physical body, since You are already in his heart.*

That is not quite true. If there were not something more in the physical contact than in the inner contact, there would have been no reason for me to take a body upon earth.<span class='page-number' id='s-65' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/65.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.65]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 October 1934
# /cwm/17/25-october-1934


## 25 October 1934

*You wrote to me: "Making an effort consists in refusing to do anything that leads you away from the Divine." I have thought about this, but I don't understand it.*

Every time I answer one of your questions, you tell me that you don't understand my reply. What to do? You must learn to reflect a little and enter into a deeper kind of thought.

Y[^1] has just written to me about the great number of novels you read. I do not think that this kind of reading is good for you—and if it is to study style, as you told me, an attentive study of one good book by a good author, done carefully, teaches much more than this hasty and superficial reading.<span class='page-number' id='s-65' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/65.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.65]</a></span>

[^1]: The Ashram librarian.


# Chapter: 25 October 1934
# /cwm/17/25-october-1934-1


## 25 October 1934

*O Mother, what shall I do? I try to understand but I don't succeed. It is the same with my studies.*

It is because your mind has not been sufficiently trained in the discipline of study.<span class='page-number' id='s-65' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/65.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.65]</a></span>

*I had two reasons for reading novels, to learn words and style.*

In order to learn you must read with great care and carefully choose what you read.<span class='page-number' id='s-66' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/66.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.66]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 October 1934
# /cwm/17/26-october-1934


## 26 October 1934

*Mother, what is this discipline I must learn in order to understand better?*

The discipline of intellectual study as it is practised in colleges in France. You can talk to Z about it; he will explain it to you.

*There is a good writer in Gujarati—I could study his books. X told me that his style is like Anatole France's.*

Really! If he writes like Anatole France he must truly be a marvellous writer!<span class='page-number' id='s-66' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/66.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.66]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 October 1934
# /cwm/17/26-october-1934-1


## 26 October 1934

*Since my illness was imaginary, it is beyond my mental capacities to understand why You gave me permission to take Sudarshan.[^1]*

[^1]: An Ayurvedic medicine.

Because your body did not know that the illness was imaginary, and it needed a remedy in order to believe in the possibility of being cured.<span class='page-number' id='s-66' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/66.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.66]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 October 1934
# /cwm/17/30-october-1934


## 30 October 1934

*Is it good to be "obliging" or to help other people?*<span class='page-number' id='s-66' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/66.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.66]</a></span>

It is certainly better to be obliging than to be intensely selfish. But even in being obliging one should observe moderation.

*At the moment there is not a single psychic element in my activity. O Mother, let nothing in me consent to lower activities.*

Yes, you must never yield to the lower nature, not only when it manifests in you but also when it manifests in others. Never listen to bad advice, never follow bad examples, never accept any other influence than that of the Divine, and your uneasiness will disappear.<span class='page-number' id='s-67' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/67.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.67]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 October 1934
# /cwm/17/30-october-1934-1


## 30 October 1934

*X is the only one who gives me advice and sets an example and I am under his influence.*

It makes little difference from whom the influence comes; do not accept it.

*This morning X asked me to tell him whenever I feel depressed.*

I see no use in speaking about your depressions to other people. It can help neither you nor them.<span class='page-number' id='s-67' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/67.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.67]</a></span>


# Chapter: 31 October 1934
# /cwm/17/31-october-1934


## 31 October 1934

*O Mother, what should I do? I am completely unconscious. Mother, where are You?*

In your psychic being—I am always present there. It is there that you can find me and must find me, and when you have found<span class='page-number' id='s-67' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/67.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.67]</a></span> me there, in the depths of your heart, you will also recognise me in my physical form.<span class='page-number' id='s-68' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/68.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.68]</a></span>


# Chapter: 31 October 1934
# /cwm/17/31-october-1934-1


## 31 October 1934

*But how can I enter the psychic centre when there is a black veil between the psychic and the integral being? (The Mother substituted the word "external" for "integral" and commented:)*

*Integral* means complete, entire, omitting nothing, total the external being is very far from being integral. When we speak of "the integral being", we mean the being in its totality, from the physical body to the true Self, the Divine Consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-68' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/68.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.68]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 November 1934
# /cwm/17/1-november-1934


## 1 November 1934

*You write "the true Self, the Divine Consciousness"—does that mean the true soul, the psychic?*

No, it is not the same thing. In several of his messages Sri Aurobindo has explained the difference between the psychic being, which is the divine element in man, and the states of being that belong to the overhead regions. Study Sri Aurobindo's messages and books a little (instead of reading novels)—then you won't ask me unnecessary questions.<span class='page-number' id='s-68' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/68.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.68]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 November 1934
# /cwm/17/1-november-1934-1


## 1 November 1934

*Of course, it is natural that I am very far away from You. First I must have a true attitude towards You and a perfect opening—which I lack. O Mother, where are You, and where am I?*

You are not so far from me as you think. You have only to calm the agitation of your mind and vital a little, remain a bit quiet<span class='page-number' id='s-68' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/68.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.68]</a></span> and concentrated, and at once you will find my presence within you and around you.<span class='page-number' id='s-69' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/69.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.69]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 November 1934
# /cwm/17/2-november-1934


## 2 November 1934

*Do You think I should stop reading Gujarati literature?*

It all depends on the effect that this literature has on your imagination. If it fills your head with undesirable ideas and your vital with desires, it is certainly better to stop reading this kind of books.<span class='page-number' id='s-69' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/69.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.69]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 November 1934
# /cwm/17/2-november-1934-1


## 2 November 1934

*Even when one is identified with You, is it true that one can do actions that are not consecrated to You?*

No, after identification it is impossible.<span class='page-number' id='s-69' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/69.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.69]</a></span>


# Chapter: 3 November 1934
# /cwm/17/3-november-1934


## 3 November 1934

*O Mother, I want to identify myself with You in such a way that I shall see You in every action.*

It would be more correct to say that you would be able to act only according to my will.<span class='page-number' id='s-69' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/69.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.69]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 November 1934
# /cwm/17/9-november-1934


## 9 November 1934

*Mother, I have been searching for You since yesterday evening, but I do not find You and I feel alone, without support.*

All these are false imaginations. If you told yourself, on the contrary, that I am always with you (which is true), it would help you to become conscious of my presence.<span class='page-number' id='s-69' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/69.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.69]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 November 1934
# /cwm/17/15-november-1934


## 15 November 1934

*O Mother, I am sad now because I don't believe what You tell me. But what can I do, the thing is not clear to me. This shows that I have no faith in You. Of course, I still have many things to learn.*

You have *everything*, absolutely everything still to learn. Above all you have to educate a mind that is still raw, ignorant and obscure, and has all the impudence of ignorance.

*O Thou, whom we must know, understand, realise...*

The first thing you must do is to learn a little humility and to recognise that you know *nothing*—you read words, you read prayers, and you repeat the words, you copy the prayers, but *you do not understand them*; you mix up all these ideas and notions in a brain that is still like a child's, and then you have the illusion of understanding!<span class='page-number' id='s-70' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/70.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.70]</a></span>


# Chapter: 3 December 1934
# /cwm/17/3-december-1934


## 3 December 1934

*On the days when I do not study, I feel uneasy. But when I begin to study, happiness comes. I don't understand this process.*

What do you mean by process? It is not a process; the disappearance of the uneasiness is the very natural result of concentrating the mind on study, which on the one hand provides it with a healthy activity, and on the other draws its attention away from this morbid contemplation of the little physical ego.<span class='page-number' id='s-70' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/70.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.70]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 December 1934
# /cwm/17/4-december-1934


## 4 December 1934

*O Mother, where are the joy and the love that filled my whole being last night during meditation? I have never known how to receive and keep what You give me.*<span class='page-number' id='s-70' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/70.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.70]</a></span>

You know how to receive, since you feel the presence of love and joy, but you do not seem to know how to keep them. You must learn to treasure in yourself silently what you have received.<span class='page-number' id='s-71' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/71.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.71]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 December 1934
# /cwm/17/4-december-1934-1


## 4 December 1934

*Please explain to me how I lose what I receive.*

By dissipation—by throwing out, either in thoughts, words or actions, the force and energy you have received.<span class='page-number' id='s-71' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/71.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.71]</a></span>


# Chapter: 7 December 1934
# /cwm/17/7-december-1934


## 7 December 1934

*I have the idea that the divine peace will not reign over the whole of the earth.*

What do you know about it? Can your mind have any knowledge of the future? And especially the supramental future!<span class='page-number' id='s-71' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/71.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.71]</a></span>


# Chapter: 8 December 1934
# /cwm/17/8-december-1934


## 8 December 1934

*This morning I told Y that Mother had told me that She does not know what will happen to this Ashram in the future. "How is it possible?" he said, "I cannot believe that She knows nothing about the work for which she has taken a body on earth."*

I do not think that I said any such thing. You must have misunderstood me. But Y is wrong to believe that I came upon earth to establish an Ashram! That would really be a very paltry objective.<span class='page-number' id='s-71' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/71.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.71]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 December 1934
# /cwm/17/10-december-1934


## 10 December 1934

*Mother, will You explain how looking at pictures can be harmful?*<span class='page-number' id='s-71' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/71.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.71]</a></span>

Naturally it depends on what the pictures are; but most often they are concerned only with things of the ordinary life and so they draw the consciousness towards that.<span class='page-number' id='s-72' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/72.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.72]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 December 1934
# /cwm/17/13-december-1934


## 13 December 1934

*O Mother, my sweet Mother, when shall I become one with You, when shall I live in You and for You?*

You must will with persistence, but not get impatient. Through calm determination you will achieve it more quickly. By getting restless, one wastes more time than one saves.<span class='page-number' id='s-72' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/72.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.72]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 December 1934
# /cwm/17/13-december-1934-1


## 13 December 1934

*Mother, is it good to go to Z's house to read the poems he has written in Gujarati?*

It all depends on the effect it has on you. If you come away feeling more peaceful and content, it is all right. If, on the contrary, it makes you feel melancholy and dissatisfied, it would be better not to go there. You have only to observe and see how it affects you, then decide accordingly.<span class='page-number' id='s-72' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/72.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.72]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 December 1934
# /cwm/17/18-december-1934


## 18 December 1934

*May I know, Mother, the conditions for the Supermind to descend in me? When I heard that the Supermind would descend in a relatively short time, I felt extremely happy.*

It is better not to speak of these things. All sincere spiritual effort towards an increase of consciousness is a preparation.<span class='page-number' id='s-72' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/72.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.72]</a></span>


# Chapter: 19 December 1934
# /cwm/17/19-december-1934


## 19 December 1934

*Will You explain why the joy and love in me get attacked by obscurity? I am not aware of having done anything, and it is not possible for the happiness and love to withdraw for no reason.*

No, nothing withdraws; it is the physical being which is unable, by nature, to hold the joy and love for very long, unless it is completely governed by the psychic.

*It is only after getting up that my condition changes.*

Yes, it is particularly at night that the physical being falls into obscurity and unconsciousness.
