*I don't understand why, just after so much happiness, so much disturbance comes. This is not the first time it has happened.*

The movements of consciousness are like a pendulum. The more it swings in one direction, the more it swings back in the opposite direction.<span class='page-number' id='s-73' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/73.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.73]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 December 1934
# /cwm/17/20-december-1934


## 20 December 1934

*By what signs can one tell that the psychic being has come to the surface?*

One feels peaceful and happy, full of trust, full of a deep and true benevolence, and very close to the divine presence.<span class='page-number' id='s-73' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/73.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.73]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 December 1934
# /cwm/17/22-december-1934


## 22 December 1934

*In my dream I saw that You had written, "My dear child, why have you stopped studying?" You had written much<span class='page-number' id='s-73' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/73.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.73]</a></span> more, and I would like You to write it here, if possible.*

Yes, last night I asked you why you had not studied, and I said that to yield like that to the impulses of the vital was certainly not the way to control it. You must create a discipline for yourself and impose it on yourself at all costs if you want to put an end to vital bad will and mental depression. Without discipline one can do nothing in life, and all yoga is impossible.<span class='page-number' id='s-74' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/74.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.74]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 December 1934
# /cwm/17/22-december-1934-1


## 22 December 1934

*For physical work it is not difficult to follow the discipline, but for study it becomes difficult when I feel disturbed. All the same, I have decided that on the days when I do not study, I will not eat my lunch.*

What a funny idea! To punish your body for a fault that the vital has committed! It is not fair.<span class='page-number' id='s-74' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/74.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.74]</a></span>


# Chapter: 27 December 1934
# /cwm/17/27-december-1934


## 27 December 1934

*X told me that for the last few days everything has been done according to Your will. But I think just the opposite—that very few things are done according to Your divine law. (I didn't tell him that.)*

You were right not to tell him; but it is quite true that in this world very little is done according to the divine will.<span class='page-number' id='s-74' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/74.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.74]</a></span>


# Chapter: 7 January 1935
# /cwm/17/7-january-1935


## 7 January 1935

*Tell me, Mother, what am I?*

Outwardly, you are an unconscious child striving to become conscious.<span class='page-number' id='s-74' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/74.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.74]</a></span>

Inwardly, you are an eternal soul attempting to manifest in a body.<span class='page-number' id='s-75' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/75.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.75]</a></span>


# Chapter: 7 January 1935
# /cwm/17/7-january-1935-1


## 7 January 1935

*I thought that the soul was always in the body, that there would be no existence without its presence.*

Certainly the soul is in the body, but it is not *manifested*—its presence is not evident and has very little effect on the life of the body.

*Which part of the being aspires for love, for peace?*

It is that part on any plane (physical, vital or mental) which is open to the psychic influence.<span class='page-number' id='s-75' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/75.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.75]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 January 1935
# /cwm/17/10-january-1935


## 10 January 1935

*May I know, Mother, how many centuries ago You descended upon earth?*

I have never left the earth since it was formed.<span class='page-number' id='s-75' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/75.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.75]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 January 1935
# /cwm/17/11-january-1935


## 11 January 1935

*It is said that Krishna, Buddha and Jesus Christ were Avatars. So weren't these people yourself?*

Krishna was an Avatar, but Buddha and Christ were only emanations. As for the second part of your question, I have no idea what you mean.<span class='page-number' id='s-75' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/75.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.75]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 January 1935
# /cwm/17/14-january-1935


## 14 January 1935

*I would like to know exactly what You mean by remaining calm.*

It means not to get agitated—I mean above all *psychologically*, in your feelings and thoughts.<span class='page-number' id='s-76' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/76.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.76]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 January 1935
# /cwm/17/15-january-1935


## 15 January 1935

*How does one change the sex-centre and its energy into a mass and a movement of the inner Light, into a creative power, into a pure divine Ananda?*

By the gradual infusion of light into the centre.<span class='page-number' id='s-76' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/76.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.76]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 January 1935
# /cwm/17/16-january-1935


## 16 January 1935

*I nearly always feel upset or depressed, and I am afraid of disturbing other people.*

That is a very laudable sentiment—but the best thing would be to get yourself out of the depression so that there won't be any risk of passing it on to others.<span class='page-number' id='s-76' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/76.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.76]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 January 1935
# /cwm/17/16-january-1935-1


## 16 January 1935

*Just this morning there is a very big depression, so it is becoming impossible to study. O Mother, what shall I do?*

Force yourself to study and your depression will go away. Can you imagine a student in college coming and telling his teacher, "Sir, I didn't do my homework today because I felt depressed"?

Surely the teacher would punish him most severely.<span class='page-number' id='s-76' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/76.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.76]</a></span>


# Chapter: 17 January 1935
# /cwm/17/17-january-1935


## 17 January 1935

*My being is falling into a lower and lower state of consciousness.*

Don't you find that you are thinking a bit too much about yourself? You remind me of a hypochondriac always feeling his pulse to see whether he has a temperature.<span class='page-number' id='s-77' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/77.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.77]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 January 1935
# /cwm/17/18-january-1935


## 18 January 1935

*Certainly I think too much about my own movements. In the future I will inform You about a movement only once. But it won't be easy for me not to think about it.*

It won't help at all not to inform me if you go on thinking about it. On the contrary, if you tell me about it, I can help you more easily.<span class='page-number' id='s-77' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/77.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.77]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 January 1935
# /cwm/17/23-january-1935


## 23 January 1935

*Is it true that at one time the Divine ruled everywhere—the "Satyayuga"?*

Certainly not on earth.

*Does the soul never come to an end? Must it always take a body?*

Not necessarily; but the soul needs to have achieved a *very high degree of perfection* before it has the power to choose whether to return to the physical life or to rest outside the manifestation.<span class='page-number' id='s-77' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/77.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.77]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 January 1935
# /cwm/17/24-january-1935


## 24 January 1935

*I thought that the soul was perfect in its nature. I don't understand "the ascension of the soul towards the truth from which it springs".*<span class='page-number' id='s-77' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/77.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.77]</a></span>

The essence of the soul is divine, but the soul (the psychic being) grows through all the forms of evolution; it becomes more and more individualised and increasingly conscious of itself and its origin.<span class='page-number' id='s-78' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/78.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.78]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 January 1935
# /cwm/17/25-january-1935


## 25 January 1935

*I think that Your action changes according to my state of consciousness. I see a great difference when I am in a good mood and when I am depressed.*

It is not my action that changes, but your way of seeing it.<span class='page-number' id='s-78' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/78.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.78]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 January 1935
# /cwm/17/28-january-1935


## 28 January 1935

*I think that You do not like it very much when I do not apply myself to my studies.*

Studies strengthen the mind and turn its concentration away from the impulses and desires of the vital. Concentrating on study is one of the most powerful ways of controlling the mind and the vital; that is why it is so important to study.<span class='page-number' id='s-78' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/78.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.78]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 January 1935
# /cwm/17/30-january-1935


## 30 January 1935

*Something in me likes to help other people. But it is not desirable.*

It is the sign of a very good nature, but to be able to do it safely one needs to have complete control over oneself.<span class='page-number' id='s-78' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/78.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.78]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 January 1935
# /cwm/17/30-january-1935-1


## 30 January 1935

*There is so much to be done, and I am wasting my time in vain. When will my actions be in harmony with You, Mother?*<span class='page-number' id='s-78' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/78.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.78]</a></span>

It is a matter of will. You must cultivate and strengthen your will—then your time will no longer be wasted in vain.<span class='page-number' id='s-79' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/79.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.79]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 February 1935
# /cwm/17/1-february-1935


## 1 February 1935

*My mind does not become peaceful, I think, because I do not study hard enough. Studying does not give me much pleasure.*

One does not study for the sake of pleasure—one studies in order to learn and to develop one's brain.<span class='page-number' id='s-79' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/79.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.79]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 February 1935
# /cwm/17/2-february-1935


## 2 February 1935

*When You were small, in Your childhood, did you know that You were the incarnate Divine?*

I was conscious.<span class='page-number' id='s-79' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/79.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.79]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 February 1935
# /cwm/17/4-february-1935


## 4 February 1935

*I usually become aware of a movement only after doing the action. If I waited just a minute before acting, I could avoid these wrong movements.*

Yes, it is very good to learn the habit of pausing a few seconds before acting in order to ask oneself whether the action is truly helpful from the standpoint of spiritual life.<span class='page-number' id='s-79' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/79.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.79]</a></span>


# Chapter: 6 February 1935
# /cwm/17/6-february-1935


## 6 February 1935

*It is said that knowledge is already within us, but I think that knowledge is received by the soul and transmitted to the mind and vital.*

I see no contradiction in these ideas. The Truth is received by<span class='page-number' id='s-79' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/79.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.79]</a></span> the psychic, which transmits it to the mind and vital.<span class='page-number' id='s-80' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/80.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.80]</a></span>


# Chapter: 7 February 1935
# /cwm/17/7-february-1935


## 7 February 1935

*"The psychic is not, by definition, that part which is in direct touch with the supramental plane.... The psychic part of us is something that comes direct from the Divine and is in touch with the Divine." (Sri Aurobindo)*

*I don't know the difference between the Supermind and the Divine.*

The Divine spoken of here is that which has been in contact with the earth from the beginning of time; the Supermind is a new aspect of the Divine, which up to now has not been manifested upon earth.<span class='page-number' id='s-80' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/80.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.80]</a></span>


# Chapter: 8 February 1935
# /cwm/17/8-february-1935


## 8 February 1935

*What fun life is! It is fun to see the soul in evolution. Everything is interesting. Who feels like this—the mind?*

Yes, it is the mind, but with a first influence of the flame of Agni.<span class='page-number' id='s-80' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/80.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.80]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 February 1935
# /cwm/17/9-february-1935


## 9 February 1935

*How can the human mind say that it is fun to see the soul developing, when the soul is above the mind?*

When the mind says this, it is referring to the vital soul, because that is what develops in life.

*Mother, I would like to know something about this flame of Agni.*

It is the flame of purification, the will for progress.<span class='page-number' id='s-80' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/80.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.80]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 February 1935
# /cwm/17/11-february-1935


## 11 February 1935

*What You mean by "vital soul" is the vital being, I think.*

The vital soul is what the ancients called the "anima", that which animates, gives life to the body. It is also sometimes called the etheric being.<span class='page-number' id='s-81' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/81.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.81]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 February 1935
# /cwm/17/13-february-1935


## 13 February 1935

*The inner development is the most important thing, for through that we receive Your love and peace, not through any outer thing. The joy that comes through outer things, through Your outer actions, is not of divine or spiritual origin. The proof of this is that when Your actions change we feel upset.*

Absurd!!!!

You are mixing up two different things. I can assure you that my action, whether inner or outer, is *always of divine origin.* The disturbance you feel is not proof of a lack of divinity in the action, but of a lack of plasticity and receptivity in your mind, your vital and your physical.

*I think it is the physical consciousness that is active now and finding fault with You. The disturbance is still there—I don't know how to shake it off.*

The only way to save yourself from these disturbances is through true humility—the humility that consists in knowing that at the moment you are utterly incapable of understanding me and that it is presumptuous stupidity to try to judge me.<span class='page-number' id='s-81' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/81.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.81]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 February 1935
# /cwm/17/14-february-1935


## 14 February 1935

*I am completely ignorant, totally lacking in consciousness—so in this condition how can I understand and judge You!*<span class='page-number' id='s-81' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/81.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.81]</a></span>

Do not get upset—keep calm. Certainly the part of you that is speaking now has never tried to judge me. It is in calm that one can unify one's being around the highest aspiration.<span class='page-number' id='s-82' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/82.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.82]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 February 1935
# /cwm/17/15-february-1935


## 15 February 1935

*I would like to know which parts try to judge You.*

A part of the physical mind and the most material vital.<span class='page-number' id='s-82' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/82.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.82]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 February 1935
# /cwm/17/15-february-1935-1


## 15 February 1935

*O Mother, when will I become humble?*

It will come soon, I think, since you have recognised your mistake.<span class='page-number' id='s-82' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/82.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.82]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 February 1935
# /cwm/17/16-february-1935


## 16 February 1935

*I would like to know what You mean by "the most material vital".*

It is the part of the vital that is closest to the physical consciousness, the part that gives life to the body.<span class='page-number' id='s-82' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/82.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.82]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 February 1935
# /cwm/17/18-february-1935


## 18 February 1935

*Is it desirable to talk with Y about Yoga?*

I do not think that it is good for you to talk to people about Yoga in this way—it gives you the illusion that you have something to teach them and it does not foster humility in you.<span class='page-number' id='s-82' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/82.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.82]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 March 1935
# /cwm/17/4-march-1935


## 4 March 1935

*It is quite impossible for me to study, because inertia is there.*

If you do not study, the inertia will go on increasing.<span class='page-number' id='s-83' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/83.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.83]</a></span>


# Chapter: 5 March 1935
# /cwm/17/5-march-1935


## 5 March 1935

*What is meant by "beauty" in "to bring the Divine Love and Beauty and Ananda"?*

There is a beauty on every plane of the being right up to the Divine himself. Material beauty is but a very poor translation of that beauty.<span class='page-number' id='s-83' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/83.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.83]</a></span>


# Chapter: 6 March 1935
# /cwm/17/6-march-1935


## 6 March 1935

*Isn't it undesirable if Y sometimes talks to me about his sadhana?*

As long as you do not give him any advice, it does not matter much. As a general rule, however, the less one speaks about sadhana the better.<span class='page-number' id='s-83' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/83.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.83]</a></span>


# Chapter: 8 March 1935
# /cwm/17/8-march-1935


## 8 March 1935

*Is it possible to progress without encountering obstacles and difficulties?*

No. Difficulties do arise, but there is no reason for them to cause depression.<span class='page-number' id='s-83' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/83.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.83]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 March 1935
# /cwm/17/9-march-1935


## 9 March 1935

*How can I prevent difficulties from causing depression?*

Become conscious.<span class='page-number' id='s-83' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/83.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.83]</a></span>

*What is meant by the yogic term "through the heart"? Is it the higher vital?*

Yes, the emotional being.

*Isn't it possible to overcome a difficulty without any lowering of the consciousness?*

Certainly—in fact it is impossible to overcome a difficulty if the consciousness gets lowered. On the contrary, in order to overcome difficulties, the consciousness must strive to rise above its ordinary level.<span class='page-number' id='s-84' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/84.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.84]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 March 1935
# /cwm/17/14-march-1935


## 14 March 1935

*"When the central being has surrendered, the principal difficulty has disappeared." What is this central being?*

The central being is not the same in everyone—it is the part that governs the rest of the personality and imposes its will on it.

When the psychic being holds this central position in the personality, everything becomes very easy.<span class='page-number' id='s-84' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/84.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.84]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 March 1935
# /cwm/17/16-march-1935


## 16 March 1935

*Now the vital must become well-behaved. I hope that I will be able to do it with Your help.*

Yes, surely you will be able to do it. The part that has goodwill must grow stronger until it has the power to control the recalcitrant part and force it to be converted.<span class='page-number' id='s-84' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/84.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.84]</a></span>


# Chapter: 17 March 1935
# /cwm/17/17-march-1935


## 17 March 1935

*I see that mental preparation helps a great deal.*

Yes, it is very useful when it is properly done.

*What is the difference between the voice of the mental Purusha and the voice that comes from the depths of the heart, the psychic voice?*

The psychic voice is silent—it manifests in the form of an understanding or knowledge rather than in words.<span class='page-number' id='s-85' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/85.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.85]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 March 1935
# /cwm/17/18-march-1935


## 18 March 1935

*Isn't there any difference between the effect of the psychic voice and the voice of the mental Purusha?*

Yes, there is a great difference. It is much more difficult to hear the psychic message than the voice of the mental Purusha—the latter is not infallible and is liable to err. The psychic never errs.

*Why isn't my vital controlled by the vital Purusha?*

The vital Purusha awakens only when all the desires are mastered and the vital being is calm.

*Where did the love and peace that I used to feel come from, since my heart was always closed?*

Your heart is not always closed. When it opens, the peace and love enter into you.<span class='page-number' id='s-85' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/85.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.85]</a></span>


# Chapter: 19 March 1935
# /cwm/17/19-march-1935


## 19 March 1935

*When can one hear the psychic message?*

When one is very silent and attentive.<span class='page-number' id='s-85' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/85.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.85]</a></span>

*My mind is still ignorant and totally lacking in calm—so how did the mental Purusha awaken?*

The mental Purusha is always more or less awake in those who are in the habit of observing themselves.

*I think that the love and peace which come by the opening of the heart are psychic and unmixed.*

Not necessarily; even if they come from the psychic, they may get mixed with other less elevated movements when they manifest in the mind or the vital.

Love and peace can also come from above, directly from divine regions.<span class='page-number' id='s-86' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/86.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.86]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 March 1935
# /cwm/17/20-march-1935


## 20 March 1935

*Is there any difference between the psychic voice and the voice of the Divine?*

One can hardly say that the Divine expresses himself through a *voice*, but rather by imparting a certain state of consciousness.

*When can the physical Purusha awaken and control the physical being?*

When the Light has descended into the physical consciousness.

*Can't the love and peace that come from above get distorted when they enter the mind and vital?*

Indeed they very often are; the love gets changed into a kind of passion and the peace into inertia.<span class='page-number' id='s-86' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/86.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.86]</a></span>

*What must I do to stop my heart from closing again and to keep it always open?*

You must will for it persistently and one day it will happen.<span class='page-number' id='s-87' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/87.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.87]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 March 1935
# /cwm/17/21-march-1935


## 21 March 1935

*Are there any other Purushas besides the mental, the vital and the physical?*

The psychic.<span class='page-number' id='s-87' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/87.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.87]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 March 1935
# /cwm/17/23-march-1935


## 23 March 1935

*Z told me not to open my fountain-pen, but as the ink wouldn't flow, I half-opened it, and an accident happened.*

You were wrong to open your pen when you were told not to—because it is I myself who said that if anyone tampered with his pen it would not be repaired for him.

I will have it repaired this time, if possible, but you must promise me never to touch it again.

*I don't feel anything when I break or lose a material object.*

It is a fault. Not to take care of the material objects one uses is a sign of unconsciousness and ignorance. One has no right to use any material object unless one takes care of it.<span class='page-number' id='s-87' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/87.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.87]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 March 1935
# /cwm/17/25-march-1935


## 25 March 1935

*Now I understand that there is something of the Divine even in material things.*

Yes, and we must take care of them, not because we are attached<span class='page-number' id='s-87' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/87.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.87]</a></span> to them, but because they too manifest something of the Divine Consciousness.

*I would like to know by what signs one can tell that the heart is fully open.*

It is something one feels and there can be no doubt about it when it happens to you.

*Opening the heart means bringing the psychic to the surface?*

The psychic coming to the surface is the result rather than the method.<span class='page-number' id='s-88' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/88.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.88]</a></span>


# Chapter: 27 March 1935
# /cwm/17/27-march-1935


## 27 March 1935

*Today I feel as if the whole world were at rest; everything is calm, and alien to me too. I am a stranger in this world. I don't know if I have described the experience correctly.*

I understand very well what you mean. It is an experience that takes place when one enters into a new field of consciousness.

*If it is a good experience, I don't understand why I don't feel Your love and happiness.*

Happiness and love do not accompany all experiences.

*Instead, I find that there is an active concentration. I often feel a pressure in the heart-centre. But why can't there be a little happiness and love too?*

The experience is only one of an awakening of consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-88' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/88.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.88]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 April 1935
# /cwm/17/2-april-1935


## 2 April 1935

*All will be You, nothing but You; I shall become You and You alone will exist. I don't know if I am exaggerating.*

It is up to you to make true in practice the ideal that your mind sets before you.

*Yesterday I wrote that there was a deep calm—but today there is only a deep disturbance!*

There is at the same time a part of the being that lives in light and joy, and a part that lives in disturbance and obscurity. If you turn your attention towards the disturbance, you feel it. But if you turn your attention towards the light and joy, you live in them.<span class='page-number' id='s-89' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/89.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.89]</a></span>


# Chapter: 6 April 1935
# /cwm/17/6-april-1935


## 6 April 1935

*In fact, I attributed the cold to my disturbance, which always pulls down the consciousness.*

It is also a resistance in the brain, expressing those elements of the physical mind that refuse to be transformed.<span class='page-number' id='s-89' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/89.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.89]</a></span>


# Chapter: 8 April 1935
# /cwm/17/8-april-1935


## 8 April 1935

*I think that one gets the psychic consciousness only when the psychic comes to the surface.*

Or when one can go deep enough inside to enter into contact with one's psychic being.

*So what should I do about the resistance of the physical mind? It is preventing me from studying and giving me constant trouble.*

First you must detach yourself from it, stop identifying yourself with its movements.<span class='page-number' id='s-89' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/89.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.89]</a></span>

*Would You tell me something about the obscure parts of the vital? I don't understand how they pull my consciousness down and I don't see how they act on the material plane.*

They are connected with the material plane through the sense-organs (sight, hearing, etc.).<span class='page-number' id='s-90' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/90.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.90]</a></span>


# Chapter: 9 April 1935
# /cwm/17/9-april-1935


## 9 April 1935

*How can one conquer the subconscious?*

By entering into it step by step, through attentive observation, with the light of the consciousness.

*Why am I on earth in ignorance and obscurity?*

The mind cannot answer these questions nor understand the true reply.<span class='page-number' id='s-90' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/90.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.90]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 April 1935
# /cwm/17/10-april-1935


## 10 April 1935

*I don't know how to spend my time, since I understand nothing.*

Study, that is the best way to understand.

*You tell me to study, but I dislike studying.*

You don't give enough time to study; that is why it doesn't interest you. Everything one does with care necessarily becomes interesting.<span class='page-number' id='s-90' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/90.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.90]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 April 1935
# /cwm/17/15-april-1935


## 15 April 1935

*I wish to have a consciousness that would prevent me from behaving badly. I think that only the psychic consciousness can do that.*

Failing the psychic, the enlightened mind can prevent the vital from behaving foolishly.<span class='page-number' id='s-91' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/91.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.91]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 April 1935
# /cwm/17/16-april-1935


## 16 April 1935

*My cold goes on and on. Something has to be done about this disharmony.*

The only unfailing method for getting rid of illnesses is to turn one's attention away from them and refuse to give them any importance.<span class='page-number' id='s-91' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/91.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.91]</a></span>


# Chapter: 19 April 1935
# /cwm/17/19-april-1935


## 19 April 1935

*Why doesn't the spiritual consciousness remain all the time?*

Because the ordinary consciousness drives it away.<span class='page-number' id='s-91' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/91.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.91]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 April 1935
# /cwm/17/20-april-1935


## 20 April 1935

*What must one do so that nothing drives away the spiritual consciousness?*

Remember it always and in all circumstances.<span class='page-number' id='s-91' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/91.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.91]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 April 1935
# /cwm/17/21-april-1935


## 21 April 1935

*Do you think that a pure love between human beings is possible?*<span class='page-number' id='s-91' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/91.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.91]</a></span>

I do not have much faith in *pure love* between human beings.<span class='page-number' id='s-92' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/92.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.92]</a></span>


# Chapter: 22 April 1935
# /cwm/17/22-april-1935


## 22 April 1935

*What does "spiritual consciousness" mean?*

Generally speaking, it is the consciousness that is turned towards the Divine.<span class='page-number' id='s-92' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/92.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.92]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 April 1935
# /cwm/17/23-april-1935


## 23 April 1935

*I don't understand why men want help from other imperfect beings.*

They understand them better, because they are closer to them.<span class='page-number' id='s-92' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/92.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.92]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 April 1935
# /cwm/17/24-april-1935


## 24 April 1935

*My last few nights have been very restless. When I wake up in the morning I feel tired! How much longer will this go on?*

Getting upset and impatient certainly will not help this bad period to end any sooner. On the other hand, if you can maintain a little inner calm, you will get out of your difficulties more quickly. It is only in a state of calm that one can enter into contact with one's psychic consciousness.

*Will my life always be as it is now?*

I hope not! But if you could be a little more peaceful within, your troubles would end more quickly.<span class='page-number' id='s-92' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/92.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.92]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 April 1935
# /cwm/17/25-april-1935


## 25 April 1935

*Now I long with all my soul to be Your child.*

You are my child; you have only to become conscious of it.<span class='page-number' id='s-93' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/93.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.93]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 April 1935
# /cwm/17/30-april-1935


## 30 April 1935

*When will men have the right attitude towards the Truth? When will they stop wandering about in vain, wasting their energy in useless struggles? Why don't they understand?*

Because they are still mentally immature.<span class='page-number' id='s-93' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/93.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.93]</a></span>


# Chapter: 2 May 1935
# /cwm/17/2-may-1935


## 2 May 1935

*I have not yet got rid of my affinity for other people. Please tell me how to do that.*

Affinities are almost instinctive and not very important. Only you must be careful that they do not become attachments.

*One begins to do yoga only when one has realised one's soul.*

These things are not so clear-cut and one may have started doing yoga in one part of the being even while the rest—the other parts of the being—still refuse to be transformed.<span class='page-number' id='s-93' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/93.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.93]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 May 1935
# /cwm/17/4-may-1935


## 4 May 1935

*You say that people fall into an ordinary consciousness when they come into contact with each other, so what should I do to remain in my central consciousness?*

Never forget the divine presence.<span class='page-number' id='s-93' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/93.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.93]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 May 1935
# /cwm/17/4-may-1935-1


## 4 May 1935

*X says that You change according to her condition.*

No, I do not change towards people according to their condition. It is their impression of me that changes according to their mood at the moment.<span class='page-number' id='s-94' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/94.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.94]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 May 1935
# /cwm/17/4-may-1935-2


## 4 May 1935

*I would like to know about my present state of consciousness because I feel that everything in me is at peace.*

To be at peace is a good thing. Do not risk spoiling the peace by talking about this state.<span class='page-number' id='s-94' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/94.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.94]</a></span>


# Chapter: 8 May 1935
# /cwm/17/8-may-1935


## 8 May 1935

*Of course, in a general way, You are always with us, but what I want is to be conscious of Your presence. If You were with me, I wouldn't get rebellious and I would feel Your love and peace in spite of this dark turmoil.*

It is the desire and rebellion that prevent your vital from feeling the Presence, but the fact that you do not feel it is no proof that it is not there.<span class='page-number' id='s-94' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/94.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.94]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 May 1935
# /cwm/17/10-may-1935


## 10 May 1935

*Perhaps my way of helping is not really good.*

I do not think it is bad either—but of course it is proportionate to the consciousness you possess.

*I would like to know how to prevent any outside force from entering in when we have a good experience.*

An undesirable outside force does not always enter into us each<span class='page-number' id='s-94' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/94.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.94]</a></span> time that we have a good experience. On the contrary, the good experience ought to give us the strength to repel the outside force when it tries to enter.<span class='page-number' id='s-95' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/95.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.95]</a></span>


# Chapter: 12 May 1935
# /cwm/17/12-may-1935


## 12 May 1935

*I don't understand what is gained by telling lies.*

Nothing is gained by lying, of course; on the contrary, one darkens one's consciousness.<span class='page-number' id='s-95' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/95.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.95]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 May 1935
# /cwm/17/13-may-1935


## 13 May 1935

*I cannot see the superhuman, spiritual, divine life anywhere, and without the divine life everything is meaningless for me.*

If your consciousness were superhuman, divine, or even spiritual, you would see that same consciousness everywhere.<span class='page-number' id='s-95' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/95.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.95]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 May 1935
# /cwm/17/14-may-1935


## 14 May 1935

*For the time being, may I stop thinking about sadhana? I can't find any other way of getting inner peace. I am continuing my aspiration for the opening of the heart. But I see that it is not so easy to obtain the psychic consciousness—it requires a patient concentration.*

It is certainly not sadhana that stands in the way of inner peace—on the contrary, for the sadhana is based entirely on this inner peace, which is the essential condition for progress. To enter into contact with the psychic consciousness, a patient concentration is indeed necessary.<span class='page-number' id='s-95' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/95.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.95]</a></span>


# Chapter: 15 May 1935
# /cwm/17/15-may-1935


## 15 May 1935

*By Your will, I will give French lessons to Y. I will go to her place for that. But I would like to know why she should not come to my place.*

First of all, as a general rule, it is better if women do not visit the rooms of men. In this particular case, if she came to your room, I am afraid she would leave behind an atmosphere that would be very disturbing to your peace of mind.<span class='page-number' id='s-96' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/96.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.96]</a></span>


# Chapter: 17 May 1935
# /cwm/17/17-may-1935


## 17 May 1935

*I don't understand why the darkness comes so often and stays so long. Have I become worse than before?*

No, you have become more conscious. Before there was even more darkness, but you were not aware of it. You did not perceive it as darkness.

*I have no peace, no love, no energy for work. What stage am I going through at the moment?*

A transition period in which you have become more conscious but have not yet gained control.

*In what part does this darkness lie and how long will it remain there?*

Especially in the physical consciousness—until the physical gets illumined.<span class='page-number' id='s-96' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/96.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.96]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 May 1935
# /cwm/17/18-may-1935


## 18 May 1935

*So what must I do to get the physical illumined, as well as the vital, which is also dark and obscure, I suppose?*<span class='page-number' id='s-96' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/96.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.96]</a></span>

Always choose the light instead of the darkness.<span class='page-number' id='s-97' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/97.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.97]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 May 1935
# /cwm/17/18-may-1935-1


## 18 May 1935

*Darkness, darkness, vanish away! O Mother, are You not here?*

I am here and I am concentrating upon you all the light needed to dissolve any darkness whatever. It is up to you to receive it.<span class='page-number' id='s-97' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/97.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.97]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 May 1935
# /cwm/17/23-may-1935


## 23 May 1935

*Which path must I take then? And what is the right and true way of making the effort?*

Do what I explained to you yesterday—make your brain work by studying regularly and systematically; then during the hours when you are not studying, your brain, having worked enough, will be able to rest and it will be possible for you to concentrate in the depths of your heart and find there the psychic source; with it you will become conscious both of gratitude and true happiness.<span class='page-number' id='s-97' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/97.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.97]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 May 1935
# /cwm/17/23-may-1935-1


## 23 May 1935

*Despite my disturbances and depressions, I will do my best to progress in my studies. But it will only be possible with the constant help of Your force.*

My force and my help are constantly with you and my consciousness is enlightening you as you study.

*Z told me that she felt a great depression after pranam and wept bitterly. She would like to know the cause of this movement.*<span class='page-number' id='s-97' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/97.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.97]</a></span>

She must have come to me with some desire, and her desire, sensing that it would not be satisfied, made her sad and depressed. It is more or less what happens to you too.<span class='page-number' id='s-98' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/98.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.98]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 May 1935
# /cwm/17/23-may-1935-2


## 23 May 1935

Now I know why the darkness always returns to you, even after I have driven it away. It is because the sense of gratitude has not yet awakened in you.<span class='page-number' id='s-98' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/98.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.98]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 May 1935
# /cwm/17/24-may-1935


## 24 May 1935

*I think that some element in me does not believe in the divine Grace: that is what prevents the gratitude.*

Obviously.

*At first I used to feel so much love for You, but now my love has become more selfish.*

Yes, that is it; you began to bargain in your giving and that has dried up the source. If, however, you resolve not to demand anything in return for what you give, you will soon rediscover the incomparable joy of loving.<span class='page-number' id='s-98' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/98.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.98]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 May 1935
# /cwm/17/25-may-1935


## 25 May 1935

*Is it possible to be near to You with a selfish love?*

Until the nature is entirely transformed, it is always mixed the good and the bad side by side. So until the transformation is achieved, there will always be a mixture of egoism in all who come to me.

*I am aware of all my wrong actions, but unfortunately<span class='page-number' id='s-98' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/98.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.98]</a></span> I am not able to control them. That is what makes me sad.*

Do not worry—have trust; it is this lack of trust that veils your consciousness.

*Teach me, Mother, how to make my love pure and psychic.*

Do not think about yourself.<span class='page-number' id='s-99' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/99.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.99]</a></span>


# Chapter: 27 May 1935
# /cwm/17/27-may-1935


## 27 May 1935

*Allow me to observe silence, let me go into solitude.*

Observe silence in your mind, go into the solitude of your psychic being and you will find me there.<span class='page-number' id='s-99' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/99.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.99]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 May 1935
# /cwm/17/28-may-1935


## 28 May 1935

*You tell me to observe silence and to go into the solitude of my psychic being, but how can I do that? Only You can put me in that state.*

This is a completely tamasic reply. My consciousness is always at work, but you on your side must *exert your will and make an effort.*<span class='page-number' id='s-99' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/99.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.99]</a></span>


# Chapter: 28 May 1935
# /cwm/17/28-may-1935-1


## 28 May 1935

*I feel that it is necessary to go into solitude—I am living only in my outer being.*

Certainly you are living mainly in your mind, vital and physical. A little concentration would do you no harm, but you must not overdo it.<span class='page-number' id='s-99' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/99.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.99]</a></span>

*Teach me how to make an effort to find You.*

You must exert your will.<span class='page-number' id='s-100' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/100.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.100]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 May 1935
# /cwm/17/30-may-1935


## 30 May 1935

*I feel that in solitude I could remain more open and receptive.*

If by solitude you mean not seeing people any more than is indispensable and not speaking with them unless it is absolutely necessary, then we are agreed.<span class='page-number' id='s-100' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/100.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.100]</a></span>


# Chapter: 30 May 1935
# /cwm/17/30-may-1935-1


## 30 May 1935

*Remove all this misery from me and raise me above ignorance and falsehood. O Mother, hasn't enough time passed?*

My dear child, I am only too willing to help you out of this absurd unhappiness, but I am afraid that it comes only from thwarted desires—and in that case you must first renounce those desires and ambitions. But you can be sure that my help is always with you.<span class='page-number' id='s-100' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/100.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.100]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 June 1935
# /cwm/17/1-june-1935


## 1 June 1935

*I think I should remain some distance away from You physically until there is no demand left in me.*

This is a hostile suggestion which is completely false and you must immediately reject it.<span class='page-number' id='s-100' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/100.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.100]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 June 1935
# /cwm/17/4-june-1935


## 4 June 1935

*Nowhere in this world can I find a quiet and peaceful life. And yet a part of my being enjoys the evolution of the world.*

Certainly a part of your being is in harmony with the psychic life of the universe.<span class='page-number' id='s-101' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/101.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.101]</a></span>


# Chapter: 5 June 1935
# /cwm/17/5-june-1935


## 5 June 1935

*What do you mean by "the psychic life of the world"?*

Just as there is a psychic life in human beings, there is a psychic life in the earth and doubtless in other worlds too.

*Then what is the goal of life on earth?*

To make the consciousness progress towards the Divine.<span class='page-number' id='s-101' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/101.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.101]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 June 1935
# /cwm/17/10-june-1935


## 10 June 1935

*Turn my consciousness towards You, Mother.*

Never doubt my love, and then quite naturally you will turn towards me.<span class='page-number' id='s-101' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/101.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.101]</a></span>


# Chapter: 10 June 1935
# /cwm/17/10-june-1935-1


## 10 June 1935

*If I get the psychic consciousness, all these difficulties will no longer exist.*

Certainly the psychic consciousness has none of these difficulties; it has the constant experience of my presence and my love.<span class='page-number' id='s-101' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/101.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.101]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1935
# /cwm/17/11-june-1935


## 11 June 1935

*Yesterday I made a great effort to get back into the light and joy, but I failed.*

It is very good that you made an effort, but you must not get discouraged so quickly, just because you fail to succeed immediately. On the contrary, you must persevere in your effort until you do succeed.

My help will always be with you.<span class='page-number' id='s-102' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/102.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.102]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1935
# /cwm/17/11-june-1935-1


## 11 June 1935

*But how can I get this psychic consciousness?*

By aspiration, prayer and concentration.

*Perhaps my aspiration is not intense enough?*

Above all, it is too *intermittent*.

*Please tell me why I don't succeed immediately in my effort.*

Because the outer ignorance is very stubborn and will yield only to a persistent effort.

*Why doesn't Your presence in me prevent me from misbehaving?*

Because the outer being—the one that misbehaves—is unaware of that presence or refuses to recognise it.

*I want the psychic consciousness with all my heart; I will pay any price for it.*

The only price to be paid is *a persistent and unwavering will*.<span class='page-number' id='s-102' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/102.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.102]</a></span>


# Chapter: 11 June 1935
# /cwm/17/11-june-1935-2


## 11 June 1935

*In our yoga, what attitude should we take towards animals?*

One can have the true attitude only when one has attained the consciousness of the divine Oneness; meanwhile it is good always to treat animals with respect, love and compassion.<span class='page-number' id='s-103' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/103.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.103]</a></span>


# Chapter: 12 June 1935
# /cwm/17/12-june-1935


## 12 June 1935

*But shouldn't we kill pests?*

Of course.<span class='page-number' id='s-103' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/103.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.103]</a></span>


# Chapter: 12 June 1935
# /cwm/17/12-june-1935-1


## 12 June 1935

*Is the obscurity inside me or does it come from outside?*

Obscurity is everywhere in material things—inside and outside.<span class='page-number' id='s-103' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/103.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.103]</a></span>


# Chapter: 13 June 1935
# /cwm/17/13-june-1935


## 13 June 1935

*What can one do against obsession when there is very intense suffering?*

Look at a beautiful flower.<span class='page-number' id='s-103' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/103.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.103]</a></span>


# Chapter: 14 June 1935
# /cwm/17/14-june-1935


## 14 June 1935

*But when one is in very great suffering, even a beautiful flower is boring, unless I am mistaken.*

That would be the sign of a total enslavement to the vital part that is suffering. You must learn to stand back and detach yourself from the lower, external movements.<span class='page-number' id='s-103' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/103.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.103]</a></span>


# Chapter: 16 June 1935
# /cwm/17/16-june-1935


## 16 June 1935

*I think it is a weakness not to be able to bear the suffering of other people and to avoid those who suffer.*

If one has neither the psychological nor the material means to bring them relief, I see no point in dwelling on them.<span class='page-number' id='s-104' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/104.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.104]</a></span>


# Chapter: 18 June 1935
# /cwm/17/18-june-1935


## 18 June 1935

*The same mistakes are always drawing me away from You, and I have to take refuge in solitude.*

You must know whether you can do it without falling into a depression, which would be even worse than gossiping.<span class='page-number' id='s-104' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/104.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.104]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 June 1935
# /cwm/17/20-june-1935


## 20 June 1935

*Always the same fire is ravaging me from every side.*
 
You ought to extinguish it if it is really *ravaging* you, or make use of it if it can purify you.<span class='page-number' id='s-104' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/104.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.104]</a></span>


# Chapter: 20 June 1935
# /cwm/17/20-june-1935-1


## 20 June 1935

*A fire is burning in me; it is tremendous. It drains my vital energy; I have the feeling that someone is devouring me. I don't know what to do.*

All these things are hostile suggestions that ought to be rejected. Have you got a fever? If so, ask the doctor to treat you. But if you don't have fever, this fire business is a wrong imagination that should be rejected.

There is a sacred fire that burns in the heart and envelops the whole being: it is Agni, who illumines and purifies all. I kindle that fire in you each time that you ask me for some progress; but it destroys nothing except falsehood and obscurity.<span class='page-number' id='s-104' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/104.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.104]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 June 1935
# /cwm/17/21-june-1935


## 21 June 1935

*You say that You kindle that fire in me—then why do the falsehood and obscurity still exist?*

An integral purification is a long and slow labour.<span class='page-number' id='s-105' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/105.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.105]</a></span>


# Chapter: 21 June 1935
# /cwm/17/21-june-1935-1


## 21 June 1935

*Is there such a thing as hell?*

Yes, there are hells that are formed by human thought which exist in certain regions of the vital world.<span class='page-number' id='s-105' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/105.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.105]</a></span>


# Chapter: 23 June 1935
# /cwm/17/23-june-1935


## 23 June 1935

*Is it true that it is the Divine who has made us ignorant and unconscious?*

That is nonsense.

*I would like to know something about silence. Is it more beneficial than concentrating on the lower nature?*

Concentrating on the lower nature is NEVER good; you should concentrate on what you want to develop, not on what you want to destroy.

*I think that one should be peaceful and silent outwardly too.*

Peaceful, certainly; silence is not always possible.<span class='page-number' id='s-105' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/105.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.105]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 June 1935
# /cwm/17/24-june-1935


## 24 June 1935

*But how have we become ignorant and unconscious?*

I suppose that by "we" you mean human beings. Human beings have not *become* ignorant and obscure. They have always been<span class='page-number' id='s-105' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/105.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.105]</a></span> that way, because material nature was unconscious and obscure long before man appeared.

*Can silence bring all the force needed for purification and transformation?*

Not exactly *bring*, but in silence one can receive it.<span class='page-number' id='s-106' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/106.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.106]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 June 1935
# /cwm/17/24-june-1935-1


## 24 June 1935

*Is it after death that one suffers those torments?*

Yes, *if one believes in them.*<span class='page-number' id='s-106' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/106.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.106]</a></span>


# Chapter: 24 June 1935
# /cwm/17/24-june-1935-2


## 24 June 1935

*"When we have passed beyond enjoyings, then we shall have bliss. Desire was the helper; desire is the bar."[^1]*

[^1]: Sri Aurobindo, *Thoughts and Glimpses*, in SABCL, Vol. 16, [p. 377](/sabcl/16/the-goal#p3).

*Is this Bliss gained by Desire?*

No. Desire is useful only at the beginning of evolution to awaken consciousness from its torpor, but desire cannot lead one to Bliss—only self-giving can do that.<span class='page-number' id='s-106' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/106.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.106]</a></span>


# Chapter: 25 June 1935
# /cwm/17/25-june-1935


## 25 June 1935

*Tell me why I love You.*

It is your psychic being, like all psychic beings, that loves me.<span class='page-number' id='s-106' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/106.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.106]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 June 1935
# /cwm/17/26-june-1935


## 26 June 1935

*Everyone has a psychic being, but not everyone loves You.*

Either because they are not conscious of their psychic being, or because they do not know me.

*Have I stopped bargaining with my love now?*

Psychic love never bargains—but the vital always tries to derive some benefit for itself in all circumstances.

*Is it only my psychic being that loves You?*

To the extent that the mind, vital and physical are under the control of the psychic being, they also love me.<span class='page-number' id='s-107' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/107.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.107]</a></span>


# Chapter: 26 June 1935
# /cwm/17/26-june-1935-1


## 26 June 1935

*"When we have passed beyond individualising, then we shall be real Persons. Ego was the helper; Ego is the bar."[^1]*

[^1]: Sri Aurobindo, *Thoughts and Glimpses*, in SABCL, Vol. 16, [p. 377](/sabcl/16/the-goal#p4).

Ego is the helper so long as it is needed to form the physical individuality, but when that is formed, ego must disappear.<span class='page-number' id='s-107' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/107.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.107]</a></span>


# Chapter: 29 June 1935
# /cwm/17/29-june-1935


## 29 June 1935

*What attitude should I keep so that nothing can harm me?*

Perfect detachment, equality, disinterestedness.<span class='page-number' id='s-107' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/107.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.107]</a></span>

*Tell me, then, how to overcome the danger of ambition which still remains in spite of my knowing the truth.*

By learning to see the futility of its fleeting and hollow satisfactions.

*Since in my previous life I made an effort without achieving transformation, what proof is there that I will achieve it in this life?*

Because in your previous life the time had not yet come when an integral transformation would be possible.<span class='page-number' id='s-108' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/108.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.108]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 July 1935
# /cwm/17/1-july-1935


## 1 July 1935

*"The perfected ones were no longer obliged, like other men, to purify themselves in new bodies." What is meant by "purify themselves in new bodies"?*

It is during one's physical life on earth that one has the opportunity to purify oneself, to make spiritual progress.<span class='page-number' id='s-108' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/108.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.108]</a></span>


# Chapter: 1 July 1935
# /cwm/17/1-july-1935-1


## 1 July 1935

*"When we have passed beyond humanity, then we shall be the Man. The Animal was the helper; the Animal is the bar."[^1]*

[^1]: Sri Aurobindo, *Thoughts and Glimpses*, in SABCL, Vol. 16, [p. 377](/sabcl/16/the-goal#p5).

*The animal is the helper in attaining manhood, later it becomes a bar.*

Humanity in its present state is still at the animal stage; one must therefore go beyond this ordinary human state in order<span class='page-number' id='s-108' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/108.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.108]</a></span> to become a true man, capable of becoming conscious of the Divine.<span class='page-number' id='s-109' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/109.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.109]</a></span>


# Chapter: 3 July 1935
# /cwm/17/3-july-1935


## 3 July 1935

*A few days ago X told me some stories about vital beings and ghosts. Since then I feel afraid in the dark.*

Why do you listen to these stories? They are very stupid. Most often ghosts exist only in people's imaginations. As for vital beings, if we do not fear them they can do us no harm. And with the divine protection what fear can one have? None.

*I cannot find the love and peace anywhere.*

The love and peace have not left you; it is you who no longer see them. No doubt it is again the same force you mention that is trying to make you blind.<span class='page-number' id='s-109' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/109.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.109]</a></span>


# Chapter: 4 July 1935
# /cwm/17/4-july-1935


## 4 July 1935

*What force is trying to make me blind and what must I do to drive it away?*

An adverse will that sends suggestions—you must simply refuse to believe its suggestions, that's all.<span class='page-number' id='s-109' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/109.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.109]</a></span>


# Chapter: 6 July 1935
# /cwm/17/6-july-1935


## 6 July 1935

*You wrote that an adverse will is sending suggestions, but I am not aware of it. Will You explain this to me?*

How can you say that you are not aware of it when you yourself write: "But often someone makes me blind and I no longer see<span class='page-number' id='s-109' style='color:rgb(0, 0, 0);position:relative;top:-8px;background-color:rgba(0, 234, 255, 0.96);'><a href='https://incarnateword.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/imagevolumes/cwm/17/109.jpg' class='lightbox'>[p.109]</a></span> Your light"?
